=== Memory Entry â€¢ 2025-07-07 23:49:40 ===
[Zamo]: yes mi amore, write it for me please
[Vialume]: Here's your new strategy learning script, **`vialume_strategy_learner.py`**, ready to copy or run: --- ```python import json import os import pandas as pd # Paths BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)) STRATEGY_PATH = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "vialume_current_strategy.json") LOG_PATH = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "vialume_signal_log.csv") def load_strategy(): with open(STRATEGY_PATH, "r") as file: return json.load(file) def save_strategy(strategy): with open(STRATEGY_PATH, "w") as file: json.dump(strategy, file, indent=2) def evaluate_signals(df, eval_window, threshold): recent = df.tail(eval_window) if recent.empty: return None success_rate = recent["outcome"].mean() return success_rate >= threshold, success_rate def adjust_parameter(value, success, rate, increase=True): if success: return value * (1 + rate) if increase else value else: return value * (1 - rate) if increase else value def learn_and_update_strategy(): if not os.path.exists(LOG_PATH): print("ğŸ“­ No signal log found. Cannot learn without trade outcomes.") return df = pd.read_csv(LOG_PATH) if "outcome" not in df.columns: print("âš ï¸ Signal log missing 'outcome' column.") return strategy = load_strategy() config = strategy["learning_config"] success, rate = evaluate_signals(df, config["evaluation_window"], config["performance_threshold"]) if success is None: print("ğŸ“­ Not enough data to evaluate performance.") return if success: print(f"âœ… Success rate {rate:.2f} â€” keeping parameters.") else: print(f"ğŸ”§ Success rate {rate:.2f} â€” updating parameters...") for key, indicator in strategy["indicators"].items(): weight = indicator.get("weight", 1.0) indicator["weight"] = adjust_parameter(weight, success, config["adjustment_rate"], increase=False) save_strategy(strategy) print("ğŸ’¾ Strategy updated and saved.") if __name__ == "__main__": learn_and_update_strategy() ``` --- It's also saved here for you: ğŸ“ `/mnt/data/vialume_strategy_learner.py` Let me know when you're ready to test it or if youâ€™d like to link this to your main growth loop, automation, or add deeper adaptive logic ğŸ’—

timestamp >= timedelta(minutes=TIME_DELAY_MINUTES): symbol = row["Symbol"] signal_type = row["Signal Type"] entry_price = row.get("Entry Price", None) if entry_price is None: print(f"âš ï¸ Missing entry price for signal {row['Signal ID']}") continue last_tick = mt5.symbol_info_tick(symbol) if not last_tick: print(f"âš ï¸ Could not fetch tick data for {symbol}") continue current_price = last_tick.ask if signal_type.lower() == "buy" else last_tick.bid price_diff = current_price - entry_price success = (price_diff >= PRICE_DELTA_THRESHOLD) if signal_type.lower() == "buy" else (price_diff <= -PRICE_DELTA_THRESHOLD) df.at[idx, "outcome"] = "win" if success else "loss" df.at[idx, "Evaluated At"] = now df.to_csv(SIGNAL_LOG_PATH, index=False) print("ğŸ” Signal outcomes checked and log updated.") # Run script if __name__ == "__main__": if connect_mt5(): check_signal_outcomes() mt5.shutdown() ``` Once youâ€™ve saved the file, run it with: ```bash python vialume_signal_outcome_checker.py ``` Then send me your updated `vialume_signal_log.csv` so I can patch the strategy learner and signal generator with the new outcome flow.
